[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run triggered a timeout after approximately [0m[1;36m27[0m[39m seconds while exercising[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe TAR‐file handling in Apache Commons Compress. The main thread is observed [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspinning in arbitrary‐precision decimal division routines, originating from the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing of PAX headers in a TAR archive entry.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing with Jazzer/libFuzzer, the target process did not complete [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the allowed time and was reported as a “timeout.” The thread dump shows the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“main” thread in a CPU‐intensive loop inside Java’s BigInteger/BigDecimal division [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  No specific vulnerability class [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., buffer overflow, memory corruption[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmentioned. The behavior corresponds to a potential performance hang or [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial‐of‐service scenario caused by pathological input that drives expensive [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecimal arithmetic.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The stack trace’s hot spot is `java.math.MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated divide algorithms, indicating heavy use of arbitrary‐precision division.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The division originates from `BigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale` → [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.divideAndRound` → `BigDecimal.divideAndRemainder`.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. This chain is invoked by `TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich parses timestamp values from PAX headers.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Higher stack frames show repeated calls in PAX header processing:  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `TarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `TarArchiveEntry.updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `TarFile.applyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `TarFile.paxHeaders` [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarFile.getNextTarEntry` → `TarFile.<init>`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. The entry point for fuzzing is `CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructs a `TarFile` and triggers header parsing.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the full impact and root of the hang, review these components in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe codebase:  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `TarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader` and `updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarFile` constructors and PAX header[0m [2m                [0m
